var theGNtracking, theGNBC, getPseudoBCValues = function (theObject) {
  var arr = [], key;
  for (key in theObject) {
    if ( (key.indexOf("pseudo") > -1) && theObject.hasOwnProperty(key) ) {
      if ( key.indexOf("Price") > -1 ) {
        arr.push(28437);
      } else if ( key.indexOf("Mileage") > -1 ) {
        arr.push(28438);
      } else if ( key.indexOf("Year") > -1 ) {
        arr.push(28423);
      }
    }
  }
  return arr;
};

var QueryString = function () {
  // This function is anonymous, is executed immediately and
  // the return value is assigned to QueryString!
  var query_string = {};
  var query = window.location.search.substring(1);
  /*if(localStorage.getItem('url') !== null){
	   query = localStorage.url;
     localStorage.removeItem('url');
  }
  else{
	   query = window.location.search.substring(1);
  }*/
  var vars = query.split("&");
  for (var i=0;i<vars.length;i++) {
    var pair = vars[i].split("=");
    	// If first entry with this name
    if (typeof query_string[pair[0]] === "undefined") {
      query_string[pair[0]] = pair[1];
    	// If second entry with this name
    } else if (typeof query_string[pair[0]] === "string") {
      var arr = [ query_string[pair[0]], pair[1] ];
      query_string[pair[0]] = arr;
    	// If third or later entry with this name
    } else {
      query_string[pair[0]].push(pair[1]);
    }
  }
    return query_string;
} ();

/* track logged in users */
(function () {
    var rememberMe, userType;
    rememberMe = (function (name) {
        var cookie, arr;

        if(typeof String.prototype.trim !== 'function') {
            String.prototype.trim = function() {
                return this.replace(/^\s+|\s+$/g, '');
            }
        }

        cookie = (function (n) {
            var cs, c, i;
            cs = window.document.cookie.split(';');
            c = '';
            for (i = 0; i < cs.length; i++) {
                if (cs[i].split('=')[0].indexOf(n) !== -1) {
                    c = cs[i];
                    break;
                }
            }
            return (typeof c === 'string') ? c.trim() : c;
        }(name));
        arr = (typeof cookie === 'string') ? cookie.split('=') : [];
        arr.shift();
        return arr.join('');
    }('rememberMe'));

    userType = rememberMe.split('~').pop();
    switch (userType) {
        case 'SIY':
            s_clven.eVar25 = "Logged In - Email";
            break;
        case 'FB':
            s_clven.eVar25 = "Logged In - Facebook";
            break;
        default:
            s_clven.eVar25 = "null";
    }
}());

function readCookie(name) {
  var nameEQ = name + "=";
  var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
  for(var i=0;i < ca.length;i++) {
    var c = ca[i];
    while (c.charAt(0)==' ') c = c.substring(1,c.length);
    if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) == 0) return c.substring(nameEQ.length,c.length);
  }
  return null;
}

      s_clven.events = o;

  }

    for (var k in o) {
      s_clven['list' + k] = o[k];
    }

  }
